We live near the lighthouse, which is relatively convenient for eating and traveling. At first, I envied those who lived on the mountain. Later, I found that living on the mountain was slightly inconvenient. The snack street + supermarket are all at the foot of the mountain. The room on the south side of the island is my favorite. The scenery is good and it is convenient to travel. It seems to be the room number starting with F.
There are many places to take pictures and check in on the island. It is still very blue on a sunny day, the color of the glass sea. You must go to the top of the mountain~
Manta ray interaction is recommended, but the ocean theater only has dolphins and sea lions performances, which is not worth the price.
I half-dive to see the seabed, which is not interesting. The glass on the right is clear, but the left is not clear.

msg:First, go to the Fenjiezhou parking lot to exchange for the boat ticket. If you live on the island, you can also enjoy free parking by scanning the code.

I didn't book the popular room, but I grabbed a mountain and sea room (Z District 882). I didn't get to the island until after 4 o'clock, and I could check in when I came out of the island pier. The assigned room faces the distant sea. Although it is not a popular room, the view is not bad (Figure 4 takes a picture of the distant sea from the balcony). Then the battery car will take you directly to the mountain. The location is at the 4th station, Youfeng Pavilion. You can get there by walking a little up after getting off the bus.

There are 4 main points for battery cars on the island. You can take a general look all the way up (see the mountain climbing tour map for details). After checking in, take a rest for a while, go down for a walk, take a look at the seaside scenery, and stroll to the Moonlight Castle to take pictures.

You can bring some food up for dinner. There are also a lot of food at the pier, which is not very expensive, but basically the kind of scenic spots. It is better to use the instant noodles provided in the room with some snacks, and you can buy some cooked food and food to go to the island.

The next day, around 6 o'clock, you can see the sunrise on the sea in the room. Breakfast is just below Yuefeng Pavilion, facing the sea, with a good environment, and the food is quite good, so don't ask for too much. After breakfast, walk up the mountain for a few minutes to reach Huanxitang, which is 3 stops away. There is a monument to the Boundary Island, a mountaintop official hat, and a beautiful mountaintop sea view.

Mountain and sea room + 2 boat tickets + transportation + instant noodles + Wanglaoji, it's generally worth it. If you are not in a hurry, you can walk around slowly and be sure to stay for one night~

msg:The water quality of Bianjiezhou Island is clear, and the sea water is rich in color on a sunny day, which is worth visiting. There is a free shuttle bus from Lingshui Station to the Fenjiezhou Island Wharf. It takes about 20 minutes. There is a club reception in the visitor center. After you redeem the ferry tickets, you can go to the island in about 10 minutes. The room fee for staying in the sea fishing club covers the island fee and the cost of the island‚Äôs battery car. It costs about 300 for these two people, so the stay is quite cost-effective. Various rooms are scattered on different corners of the island. I personally feel that the Guanhai Pavilion facing the east is the most cost-effective. It is located on the top of the mountain and is relatively quiet. Sitting on the balcony can watch the sunrise and admire the endless invincible horizon. Because I booked it late, I missed the Guanhai Pavilion. I chose the cheapest Linhai Pavilion, which is right by the pier. Although the view is a bit poor, it is very close to the food court and does not need to come down from the mountain to search for food. Many guests who like fishing choose to live in this room type. You can fish from the balcony. The first floor is more convenient. Although there is no elevator, the guy at the front desk is very enthusiastic and helps to carry luggage upstairs. There is no boat at night, so it is not too noisy, but there will be the sound of waves. Fortunately, the sound insulation effect is not bad. During the day, you can see divers, crabs basking in the sun under the balcony, and you can also see fish in the sea. The room is large, the decoration style is simple, there are many sockets, and there is plenty of storage space. It is no problem to stay for a few days. The minibar is free of mineral water, Jiaduobao, tea and coffee, and two cans of Jinmailang instant noodles. This is more unpalatable. The room by the sea is unavoidable and understandable, and there is no serious discomfort. The room is very clean, but I still saw a German cockroach. Tucao a little bit, the bathroom ventilation is done well, and it also achieves the separation of dry and wet, but the floor seam between the shower room and the toilet is not properly sealed, and I don‚Äôt know if it‚Äôs just a problem in my room. The toilet next to the shower is filled with water. Man Jinshan. The service attitude of the hotel is very good, as long as there are vacancies, you can check in early, and the breakfast will be sent up the mountain by a battery car the next day. The restaurant is located on a cliff with invincible views. The food is not delicious, but the variety is good. This scenery matches the price, so I dare not ask too much. One night is enough for simply playing. Those who like diving and fishing can stay for a few more days. After all, the sea in Lingshui is still better than Sanya and Wanning.

Guests who check in before 10 pm can ride up and down the mountain for free (after 10:00, call for a car appoin**ent and pay 10 yuan/time).
The room is really big and the bathroom is also big. At night, you can watch the stars and listen to the sound of the waves on the balcony with the sea breeze (the wind is quite strong), and you can also watch the lights along the mountain pier along the mountain road. Generally, tourists leave the island after 5 or 6 in the afternoon. This is a good time for tourists residing on the island. There are still many stores open at night, and there are bonfire parties, which are very lively.
There are many different types of rooms in the hotel, and tourists should choose according to their preferences, not just the price. For example, those who like lively and convenient shopping can choose Linhai Pavilion near the pier; those who prefer privacy can choose the rainforest house in the middle of the mountain; those who like mountain and sea views can choose the sea-viewing pavilion on the cliff side of the mountain; those who like domineering sea and sky just Choose the island owner‚Äôs villa on the hill. Be sure to dine at the cliff restaurant in Decision Valley, and experience the taste of the cliffside breakfast outdoors before the sun rises above your head.
I sincerely recommend that tourists who come to Fenjiezhou Island stay here for one or two nights. They will definitely feel different and feel relieved to blend in with nature.
